### 1. 使用 Nano Banana 2 创作的高级时装大片提示词

**作者**: [Synthia](https://x.com/AIwithSynthia/status/2041374827077136438)  **日期**: 2026-04-07  **语言**: en

> 一个用于生成高级时装大片图像的提示词：一位时尚的年轻女性坐在俯瞰现代城市的屋顶上，身穿大胆的红色人造皮草外套和牛仔裤，具有电影般的构图和超逼真的细节。

![使用 Nano Banana 2 创作的高级时装大片提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775631281676_s99njb_HFRrljKa4AApv_r.jpg)

```
A stylish young woman sitting casually on the edge of a rooftop overlooking a dense modern city, wearing a bold {argument name="coat color" default="red"} faux fur coat, light blue relaxed-fit jeans, and brown leather ankle boots. She has short, slightly messy black hair and a calm, confident expression. The city below is highly detailed with streets, cars, and buildings stretching into the distance, with a famous tower visible in the background. Shot in natural daylight with soft shadows, cinematic composition, wide-angle perspective, ultra-realistic, high fashion editorial style, shallow depth of field, 8k detail.
```

### 2. Nano Banana Pro 的超写实角色参考图提示词

**作者**: [Kol Tregaskes](https://x.com/koltregaskes/status/2041252385721651401)  **日期**: 2026-04-06  **语言**: en

> 一份为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的高精度提示词，用于创建 8 宫格超写实角色参考图，展示一名身着科幻战术装备的 29 岁女性，包含布局、一致性要求及输出质量说明。

![Nano Banana Pro 的超写实角色参考图提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775544739194_vd4gve_HFP8Ob3agAA0zqK.jpg)

```
Create a photoreal character reference sheet on a pure white background.

Character:
A 29-year-old woman with a lean athletic build, short black hair with a silver streak, steel-blue eyes, a stern intelligent expression, and a lightly weathered face. She wears an asymmetrical dark graphite tactical coat with a fitted high collar, a matte black bodysuit, segmented forearm armour, a compact chest rig, a slim utility belt, fitted tactical trousers, and reinforced boots. The overall look is a modern sci-fi operative aesthetic with realistic fabric, subtle worn metal, dust, and light scratches.

Layout:
Strict 8-panel turnaround sheet.
Top row: full-body front view, full-body back view, full-body left side view, full-body right side view.
Bottom row: close-up head front view, close-up head back view, close-up head left side view, close-up head right side view.

Requirements:
Pure white background, no shadows, evenly spaced panels, highly accurate identity consistency, highly accurate facial consistency, highly accurate outfit consistency, highly accurate proportions, clean production-ready presentation, exact side views, no three-quarter views.

Pose:
Neutral standing pose, arms relaxed at sides.

Output:
Photoreal, ultra-detailed, sharp focus, no props, no weapons, no text, no labels, no logos.
```

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "subject": "Young woman with blonde hair in a messy ponytail and bangs, sweaty skin.",
    "clothing": "Light pink cropped tank top, matching light pink sweatpants.",
    "pose": "Right arm raised flexing bicep, left hand resting on hip, serious expression looking at camera.",
    "environment": "Gym interior, mirror reflection showing a rack of dumbbells and warm overhead lights.",
    "technical_specs": "4k ultra quality, highly detailed, photorealistic, 9:16 canvas aspect ratio",
    "full_prompt": "A young blonde woman with a messy ponytail, sweaty skin, wearing a pink crop top and pink sweatpants. She is flexing her right bicep with her left hand on her hip. Gym interior background with a mirror and dumbbell racks. 4k ultra quality, highly detailed, photorealistic, 9:16 canvas."

}

### 4. Nano Banana Pro 逼真图像提示词：Sabrina Carpenter 主题

**作者**: [LexiPrompt](https://x.com/Artist04048661/status/2039071678953652270)  **日期**: 2026-03-31  **语言**: en

> 一份为 Nano Banana Pro 模型设计的详细结构化 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张超逼真的 RAW 照片，画面中是一位酷似 Sabrina Carpenter 的年轻女性，身着 Y2K 运动休闲装，在黄金时段的户外泳池露台上眨眼喝饮料。

![Nano Banana Pro 逼真图像提示词：Sabrina Carpenter 主题](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1775112289227_pgir45_HEw8tx7aIAAh1o2.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman with a strong resemblance to {argument name="subject name" default="Sabrina Carpenter"}.",
      "hair": "Straight, parted middle, pinned back with clips on sides.",
      "face": "Winking, sipping straw, warm sunlit skin.",
      "body": "Slender, exposed midriff, smooth skin."
    },
    "attire": {
      "clothing": "{argument name="clothing style" default="Pink Y2K zip-up crop top and matching mini skirt with white trim"}.",
      "style": "Y2K athleisure."
    },
    "styling_and_accessories": {
      "jewelry": [
        "White hair clips",
        "Small pendant necklace",
        "Clear plastic cup with green drink",
        "Smartphone"
      ]
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "Outdoor pool patio.",
      "background": "Lounge chairs, closed blue umbrella, manicured bushes.",
      "water": "Calm, reflective blue pool water."
    },
    "pose": {
      "posture": "Standing casually, slight hip tilt.",
      "arms": "Right arm down holding phone, left arm raised holding cup.",
      "angle": "Eye-level, knee-up framing."
    },
    "lighting_and_mood": {
      "lighting": "Harsh golden hour sunlight, strong directional shadows.",
      "mood": "Warm, summery, casual.",
      "colors": "Pink, blue, golden, dark green."
    },
    "camera_and_technical": {
      "style": "Ultra Photorealistic, RAW photo.",
      "lens": "50mm",
      "aperture": "f/2.8",
      "quality_tags": [
        "8k resolution",
        "highly detailed",
        "volumetric lighting",
        "ray tracing reflections",
        "hyper-realistic texture",
        "Hasselblad photography"
      ]
    }

> 一份为 Nano Banana Pro 准备的详细提示词，旨在生成一张 Anya Taylor-Joy 的生活方式时尚大片。画面呈现“软妹邂逅运动风”的美学风格，她在黄金时刻蹲在户外篮球场上，强调严格的身份锁定和照片级真实细节。

![“软妹”运动风篮球场时尚大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774853734577_3o3kn6_HElHJlJagAAayTY.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Young woman squatting on an outdoor basketball court holding a basketball close to her face, Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact",
      "identity_lock": "STRICT — Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact. Preserve facial features, skin tone, eyes, and proportions. Do not alter identity.",
      "pose": {
        "body_position": "deep squat position with heels raised slightly",
        "legs": "knees bent fully, feet close together",
        "torso": "upright with slight forward lean",
        "arms": "one hand holding basketball near cheek, other arm relaxed near knee",
        "head_position": "tilted slightly toward ball",
        "expression": "soft confident gaze toward camera with slightly parted lips"
      }
    },
    "face_details": {
      "instruction": "Use uploaded reference image, keep identity exact",
      "expression": "confident, relaxed, slightly playful",
      "skin": "realistic texture with visible pores and natural glow from sunlight",
      "eyes": "sharp with warm sunlight reflections",
      "imperfections": "natural asymmetry and skin variation"
    },
    "hair": {
      "instruction": "Preserve hairstyle exactly",
      "style": "long straight hair falling over shoulders",
      "details": "natural movement, slight wind or softness"
    },
    "makeup": {
      "style": "natural glam",
      "skin_finish": "warm sunlit glow",
      "eyes": "light eyeliner and mascara",
      "lips": "natural glossy tone",
      "imperfection": "slightly imperfect blending for realism"
    },
    "clothing": {
      "outfit": "white fitted crop top and orange athletic shorts",
      "footwear": "clear high-heeled shoes with socks",
      "accessories": "bracelets and glasses",
      "details": "natural fabric folds, slight stretch"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "outdoor basketball court",
      "surface": "reddish court with white curved line markings",
      "props": "basketball with visible branding",
      "background": "trees, fence posts, and soft blurred park environment"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "golden hour sunlight",
      "style": "warm directional light from side",
      "effect": "strong warm highlights and soft long shadows",
      "shadows": "soft elongated shadows on ground",
      "imperfections": "slight overexposure on highlights"
    },
    "camera": {
      "type": "digital camera",
      "lens": "50mm",
      "angle": "slightly low angle at subject level",
      "distance": "medium full-body framing",
      "focus": "sharp on subject with soft background blur",
      "imperfections": "slight lens softness, natural grain"
    },

### 8. 巴塞罗那四位女性的集体自拍

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2037211829005647891)  **日期**: 2026-03-26  **语言**: en

> 一个 JSON 提示词，用于生成一张群组自拍，其中包含四位不同的个体（艾玛·斯通、安妮·海瑟薇、安娜·德·阿玛斯，以及第四个人，使用参考图像锁定身份），以休闲、随意的风格在一条欧洲城市街道上，强调广角畸变和逼真的皮肤纹理。

![巴塞罗那四位女性的集体自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774594340100_3td6m7_HEWhVuRbYAAprKm.jpg)

```
{
  "image_generation_prompt": {
    "subject": {
      "description": "Four young women taking a group selfie outdoors, Use uploaded reference images, keep identity exact for each person",
      "identity": {
        "person_1": "Use uploaded reference image 1, keep identity exact — no mixing",
        "person_2": "Use uploaded reference image 2, keep identity exact — no mixing",
        "person_3": "Use uploaded reference image 3, keep identity exact — no mixing",
        "person_4": "Use uploaded reference image 4, keep identity exact — no mixing"
      },
      "consistency_rules": "Each face must strictly match its corresponding reference image — same facial structure, eyes, nose, lips, proportions, and skin tone. No blending or identity drift.",
      "hair": {
        "person_1": "match reference image — natural strands, slight movement",
        "person_2": "match reference image — realistic texture and flyaways",
        "person_3": "match reference image — natural volume and separation",
        "person_4": "match reference image — soft realistic flow"
      },
      "face": {
        "details": "Use uploaded reference images, keep identity exact — visible pores, natural skin texture, no beautify smoothing",
        "expressions": {
          "person_1": "playful pout",
          "person_2": "winking smile",
          "person_3": "soft confident smile",
          "person_4": "side-leaning relaxed expression with closed eyes"
        }
      },
      "body": "natural proportions, close group pose, shoulders touching"
    },
    "attire": {
      "style": "casual streetwear / tourist outfits",
      "details": "simple tops, neutral tones, minimal branding, realistic fabric wrinkles and folds"
    },
    "composition": {
      "type": "group selfie",
      "framing": "tight upper-body framing with slight wide-angle distortion",
      "arrangement": "four faces close together, slightly overlapping, filling frame",
      "camera_position": "held by one subject at arm’s length"
    },
    "environment": {
      "setting": "European city street (Barcelona-style architecture)",
      "background": "ornate historic building with balconies and stone details, slightly blurred depth",
      "details": "tourist environment, soft crowd presence, urban textures"
    },
    "lighting_and_mood": {
      "lighting": "natural daylight, soft diffused light with slight directional highlights",
      "effects": "even skin tones, subtle shadows, realistic outdoor color balance",
      "mood": "fun, friendly, travel lifestyle, candid"
    },
    "camera_and_technical": {
      "style": "smartphone selfie photography",
      "lens": "24mm wide-angle equivalent",
      "aperture": "f/1.8",
      "quality_tags": [
        "high resolution",
        "natural depth of field",
        "slight lens distortion",
        "realistic skin texture",
  "
      ]
    }
  }
}
```

### 9. 适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的随性手机照片提示

**作者**: [brindley](https://x.com/brindleyai/status/2036370453195849991)  **日期**: 2026-03-24  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示词，旨在生成一张逼真的图像，模仿日常随手拍的智能手机照片。它详细说明了主题、环境、构图、相机设置（包括深景深和平视角度）、自然光照和纹理，目标是实现一种未经修饰、逼真的快照效果。

![适用于 Nano Banana Pro 的随性手机照片提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774421487919_lb2zea_HEKkH1sacAAHtWi.jpg)

```
{
  "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
  "photo_style": "casual everyday smartphone photo",
  "subject": "A woman with long, dark, wavy hair and braids, wearing a light blue camisole, sitting at a restaurant table. She is holding a fresh green coconut with a straw in one hand and holding a small piece of fruit to her mouth with the other.",
  "environment": "An airy, upscale indoor-outdoor restaurant or resort lounge with warm wood-paneled ceilings, large white pillars, and louvered windows. The furniture includes light-colored textured seating.",
  "composition": "A centered, waist-up medium shot taken from across the table. In the foreground, there is a white coffee cup on a saucer and a ceramic plate with slices of papaya, guava, and dragon fruit.",
  "camera": {
    "angle": "Eye-level",
    "distance": "Medium-close",
    "perspective": "Point-of-view from someone sitting across the table",
    "depth_of_field": "deep focus"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "natural light",
    "source": "Ambient daylight coming from the side",
    "shadow_softness": "soft natural shadows",
    "exposure": "normal"
  },
  "color_science": {
    "style": "natural colors",
    "white_balance": "neutral",
    "contrast": "normal"
  },
  "materials_and_textures": "Rough texture of a carved green coconut, smooth ceramic plate and coffee cup, wooden ceiling slats, woven fabric on the booth seating.",
  "atmosphere": "Relaxed, casual vacation breakfast or brunch vibe.",
  "generation_prompt": "A casual smartphone photo of a woman with long wavy dark hair and braids sitting at a wooden table in a brightly lit resort restaurant. She is wearing a simple light blue top, holding a fresh coconut with a straw, and eating a piece of fruit. On the table in front of her is a white cup of coffee and a plate with sliced tropical fruits like papaya and dragon fruit. The background shows the interior of a luxury hotel with wooden ceilings and white pillars, all in clear focus. The lighting is natural daytime light with no blur or professional effects. Natural skin tones, neutral colors, 3:4 aspect ratio, everyday snapshot look."
}
```

### 10. Nano Banana Pro 复古闪光灯群拍提示词

**作者**: [glena Jenner](https://x.com/GlenaJenne/status/2034912627525349654)  **日期**: 2026-03-20  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于让 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张室内派对自拍，其中包含三个人物（Sadie Sink、Sydney Sweeney 和用户），并带有复古闪光灯美学。该提示词指定了刺眼的直射闪光灯照明、紧凑的构图、特定的表情（嘟嘴），以及可见颗粒和皮肤纹理等真实感细节，并要求提供三张参考图像以保留人物身份。

![Nano Banana Pro 复古闪光灯群拍提示词](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1774074533519_qk36kf_HD12P_ubkAAm5yR.jpg)

```
{
  "photo_type": "Indoor party selfie (vintage flash aesthetic, raw realism)",

  "subjects": [
    {
      "id": "person_left",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 1, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Leaning slightly inward, shoulder angled forward",
      "expression": "Pout lips, slightly squinted eyes, relaxed playful look"
    },
    {
      "id": "person_center",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 2, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Centered, leaning slightly forward toward camera",
      "expression": "Soft pout lips, relaxed eyes, subtle confidence"
    },
    {
      "id": "person_right",
      "face": {
        "description": "Use reference image 3, keep identity 100% unchanged"
      },
      "pose": "Leaning inward, head slightly tilted toward center",
      "expression": "Pout lips, soft playful expression"
    }
  ],

  "interaction": {
    "body_contact": "tight shoulder-to-shoulder grouping",
    "energy": "casual, playful, close friends"
  },

  "pose_rules": {
    "important": [
      "faces very close together",
      "slight overlap of shoulders",
      "tight crop composition",
      "all subjects angled toward camera"
    ]
  },

  "expression_rules": {
    "important": [
      "all subjects doing pout/kiss face",
      "slight variation in intensity",
      "natural not exaggerated"
    ]
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "direct harsh flash",

    "setup": [
      "camera flash from front",
      "dark indoor environment",
      "no soft lighting"
    ],

    "effects": [
      "bright face highlights",
      "flat lighting on skin",
      "strong shadow falloff behind",
      "flash shine on nose and cheeks"
    ],

    "color_temperature": "warm slightly orange tint"
  },

  "camera": {
    "type": "smartphone front camera",

    "lens": "24mm wide",

    "settings": {
      "aperture": "f/2.2",
      "iso": "ISO 700",
      "shutter_speed": "1/60s"
    },

    "lens_behavior": [
      "slight wide distortion",
      "faces closer appear slightly larger",
      "edge softness"
    ],

    "sensor_behavior": [
      "visible grain",
      "color noise",
      "low dynamic range",
      "flash overexposure in highlights"
    ]
  },

  "color_grading": {
    "style": "vintage digital",

    "rules": [
      "warm orange tone",
      "slightly faded blacks",
      "film-like softness",
      "no modern HDR look"
    ]
  },

      "natural texture"
    ]

### 17. 动物练习人类技能图片生成模板

**作者**: [Gadgetify](https://x.com/Gdgtify/status/2031023956229279783)  **日期**: 2026-03-09  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana 设计的复杂多步骤提示模板，用于生成动物进行人类活动的逼真、坦率的训练瞬间，例如猫练习空手道或狗举重。该提示包含技能转移、场景容器、动作、真实性限制和视觉语法等方面的详细说明。

```
<instruction>   Do this for [Animal / Creature / Pet] practicing [Human Skill / Martial Art / Discipline]:  

1. Skill Transfer: 
Input A is an animal or creature.
Input B is a human discipline, martial art, craft, sport, or skill.

Analyze both inputs and infer:

Species Motion Traits: the natural posture, balance, limb movement, paw/wing/claw use, and body proportions of Input A.

Discipline Mechanics: the essential movement or technique associated with Input B (stance, strike, block, craft motion, or tool use).

Training Interaction: determine how a human trainer, instructor, or environment would realistically guide or test the skill.

Scale & Equipment: infer the correct training props, uniforms, or equipment sized appropriately for the animal.

2. Container 
Goal: a believable practice or training scene.

The environment should be the natural location where the discipline would occur:

dojo, gym, workshop, field, training hall, studio, kitchen station, laboratory bench, etc.

The environment should contain recognizable training objects or equipment relevant to Input B.

3. Scene 

Input A actively performs the discipline in a recognizable stance or action.

A trainer, instructor, or observer may assist by holding equipment, guiding posture, or presenting a challenge (such as a target or object).

The moment should capture the key action of the skill: striking, crafting, balancing, lifting, cutting, shaping, blocking, or demonstrating technique.

4. Realism Constraint:

preserve realistic anatomy of Input A (fur patterns, whiskers, paws, tail movement, posture).

any clothing or gear must support the activity rather than dominate the scene (training belt, small uniform, gloves, apron, etc.).

tools and objects must be physically scaled so the action feels believable.

5. Visual Syntax

Camera: candid mid-range shot like a paused video frame or training moment

Lighting: natural indoor lighting or soft gym lighting

Detail: realistic fur, equipment textures, and environmental details

Mood: playful but believable, skill demonstration moment

6. Flexibility Constraint:
This should work for any combination such as:

cat practicing karate

dog lifting weights

raccoon woodworking

bird painting

rabbit gardening

The system must infer correct props, stance, and environment from the variable inputs without hardcoding specific animals or disciplines.

Output: ONE image, vertical or square aspect ratio, realistic candid training moment of an animal performing a human discipline with believable environment and props.
</instruction>
```

**Related**: [[手绘素描]]、[[室内设计]]、[[概念艺术]]

### 21. 超逼真的健身房锻炼场景

**作者**: [KeorUnreal](https://x.com/KeorUnreal/status/2030753511651373340)  **日期**: 2026-03-08  **语言**: en

 },

### 30. 高速摄像机急速运动提示

**作者**: [Oogie](https://x.com/oggii_0/status/2029580197696356802)  **日期**: 2026-03-05  **语言**: en

> 一段用于视频生成（Kling 3.0）的详细运动提示词，描述了一个单一的连续镜头：镜头从高处开始，向下俯冲，以快速移动和运动模糊穿过一个环境，然后急剧减速，最终聚焦在一个主体上。该提示词详细说明了摄像机运动、动作和风格，旨在营造一种惊险刺激的效果。

```
Motion Prompt: CAMERA:
Single continuous shot. The camera moves at high speed through the environment in a straight-line rush. Starts high above, then immediately dives down into the scene. The camera weaves between obstacles with tight margins — quick banking turns, rapid dodges, surroundings rushing past in peripheral blur. Light flickers rapidly through beams and shadows. Final approach decelerates sharply as the subject comes into view, the speed resolving into a calm, steady hover. Camera settles into a low-angle medium shot with subtle drift.
ACTION:
Opens from above, then plunges into the environment. Surroundings become a blur of color and light streaks. Obstacles whoosh past on both sides, particles streak through the frame. Volumetric light rays flash by. As the subject appears ahead, speed suddenly drops, chaos calms, and the camera floats the final distance. The final frame holds steady on the subject, glowing and still. Nothing is visible in the frame except the environment and the subject.
STYLE:
Thrilling high-speed camera rush. Urgent and exhilarating. Rapid light–shadow transitions with motion blur emphasizing speed. The contrast between the frenetic journey and the calm arrival creates a satisfying effect. CAMERA:
Single continuous shot. The camera moves at high speed through the environment in a straight-line rush. Starts high above, then immediately dives down into the scene. The camera weaves between obstacles with tight margins — quick banking turns, rapid dodges, surroundings rushing past in peripheral blur. Light flickers rapidly through beams and shadows. Final approach decelerates sharply as the subject comes into view, the speed resolving into a calm, steady hover. Camera settles into a low-angle medium shot with subtle drift.
ACTION:
Opens from above, then plunges into the environment. Surroundings become a blur of color and light streaks. Obstacles whoosh past on both sides, particles streak through the frame. Volumetric light rays flash by. As the subject appears ahead, speed suddenly drops, chaos calms, and the camera floats the final distance. The final frame holds steady on the subject, glowing and still. Nothing is visible in the frame except the environment and the subject.
STYLE:
Thrilling high-speed camera rush. Urgent and exhilarating. Rapid light–shadow transitions with motion blur emphasizing speed. The contrast between the frenetic journey and the calm arrival creates a satisfying effect.
```

### 34. Nano Banana Pro 健身编辑网格提示（粉色运动服）

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2029252532745158741)  **日期**: 2026-03-04  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的 JSON 提示，用于 Nano Banana Pro 模型，旨在生成一个 2x2 的编辑网格，展示一位女运动员穿着鲜艳的粉色运动服摆出各种姿势。它对解剖结构、手部和输出设置规定了严格的质量控制，并使用图像到图像模式作为布局灵感。

![Nano Banana Pro 健身编辑网格提示（粉色运动服）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692214345_n6wgfd_HClaW1PXIAEzB2H.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "fitness_editorial_grid_variations",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v2.0_PINK_ACTIVEWEAR_EDITORIAL_GRID"
    },

    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "high",
      "preserve_layout": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference image only as layout inspiration for a fitness editorial collage. Create new poses and a different outfit design. No logos or text."
    },

    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin"
      },
      "sharpness": "editorial_crisp"
    },

    "scene": {
      "environment": "clean minimal fitness studio with soft neutral background",
      "lighting": "soft commercial studio lighting"
    },

    "wardrobe": {
      "color": "vibrant pink activewear",
      "styles": [
        "pink asymmetric sports bra with high waist leggings",
        "pink cropped zip jacket with biker shorts",
        "pink seamless workout set with mesh panels",
        "pink athletic bodysuit with cutout details"
      ],
      "material": "premium matte compression fabric"
    },

    "poses": [
      "athlete stretching arms overhead",
      "dynamic lunge pose",
      "side profile standing power pose",
      "kneeling pose holding workout ball"
    ],

    "subject": {
      "type": "female athlete",
      "body": "fit athletic physique",
      "hair": "sporty ponytail or loose waves",
      "makeup": "natural sporty glow"
    },

    "anatomy_rules": {
      "realistic_joint_angles": true,
      "correct_muscle_tension": true,
      "balanced_body_weight": true
    },

    "hand_integrity": {
      "five_fingers_each_hand": true,
      "natural_finger_spacing": true,
      "no_extra_fingers": true,
      "no_missing_fingers": true
    },

    "quality_control": {
      "avoid": [
        "text",
        "watermark",
        "brand logos",
        "distorted anatomy",
        "extra limbs",
        "extra fingers",
        "blur"
      ]
    },

    "negative_prompt": [
      "text",
      "logo",
      "watermark",
      "extra fingers",
      "missing fingers",
      "distorted anatomy",
      "low resolution",
      "blurry"
    ]
  }
}

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2029252037074923702)  **日期**: 2026-03-04  **语言**: en

> 这是一个针对 Nano Banana Pro 模型的高度具体的 JSON 提示，旨在生成一个 2x2 的编辑健身拼贴画，其中所有四个画面都展现同一位女性运动员。它指定了四种不同的姿势、浅柔和的黄色运动服主题，并对解剖结构和手部有严格的质量控制，使用图像到图像模式来保持身份一致性。

![Nano Banana Pro 健身社论网格提示（黄色运动服，身份锁定）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772692215482_s86ypg_HClZ55iWcAARfh5.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "fitness_editorial_2x2_pose_grid_identity_locked",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v2.0_YELLOW_FITNESS_EDITORIAL_GRID"
    },

    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "maximum",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "notes": "Create a 2x2 editorial fitness collage using the four reference poses: (1) floor bicycle crunch pose, (2) deep forward fold stretch, (3) kneeling back stretch pose, (4) standing dumbbell pose. Same woman identity in all frames."
    },

    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 2,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "outer_border": "none"
      },
      "sharpness": "editorial_crisp",
      "grain": "subtle_film",
      "render_style": "premium_fitness_editorial"
    },

    "styling": {
      "outfit": {
        "top": "light pastel yellow athletic sports bra",
        "bottom": "light pastel yellow seamless leggings",
        "fabric": "matte performance fabric"
      },
      "shoes": "light pastel yellow running sneakers matching the outfit",
      "socks": "white athletic crew socks",
      "headphones": "light pastel yellow over-ear fitness headphones",
      "dumbbells": "light pastel yellow coated dumbbells",
      "color_palette": [
        "soft pastel yellow",
        "warm neutral skin tones",
        "clean studio white background"
      ]
    },

    "scene": {
      "environment": "minimal clean studio background, soft white / light beige tone",
      "lighting": "soft high-end fitness studio lighting, even highlights, clean shadows",
      "camera": {
        "lens": "50mm",
        "focus": "sharp on subject with subtle depth",
        "composition": "editorial sports campaign style"
      }
    },

    "anatomy_rules": {
      "hands_priority": "high",
      "finger_count": 5,
      "correct_thumb_orientation": true,
      "natural_muscle_definition": true,
      "no_extra_limbs": true,
      "no_distortion": true
    },

    "quality_control": {
      "avoid": [
        "logos",
        "text",
        "brand names",
        "watermark",
        "extra fingers",
        "missing fingers",
        "distorted anatomy",
        "plastic skin",
        "blurry face"
      ]
    },

      "extra limbs",
      "extra fingers",
      "missing fingers",
      "distorted hands",
      "blur",

      "cgi look"

  }

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于生成一张超逼真的年轻女性图像，她身穿 Y2K 街头服饰（印花露脐上衣、破洞超短裤、铆钉腰带），酷似阿曼达·塞弗里德 (Amanda Seyfried)。场景设定在黄昏时分的沿海公路旁，一辆鲜艳的橙色跑车旁，强调电影级灯光、高对比度和光线追踪反射。

**作者**: [Spicy Success](https://x.com/spicyysuccess/status/2028096778172776683)  **日期**: 2026-03-01  **语言**: en

> 一个 JSON 结构，分析了用于生成健身房中运动型男士图像的可能提示和特征。它详细描述了主体的服装（法兰绒衬衫、紧身短裤）、姿势（在杠铃片上比出和平手势）、环境（CrossFit 健身房）和 AI 伪影（无意义的文本、扭曲的解剖结构）。

```

    "subject": "Young athletic man with messy blonde hair, neutral expression",
    "clothing": [
      "Black and white plaid flannel shirt",
      "White tank top",
      "White compression shorts",
      "White crew socks (no shoes)"
    ],
    "pose": "Sitting on a stack of black barbell weight plates, making a peace sign",
    "environment": "Industrial CrossFit gym or warehouse weightlifting facility",

      "Large chalkboard leaderboard with handwritten workout scores",
      "Wooden Rogue plyo boxes",
      "Rubber gym flooring",
      "Dumbbells and industrial fans"
    ],
    "style": "High-resolution digital photography, social media aesthetic, bright overhead lighting",

      "Nonsensical text on the chalkboard",
      "Slightly distorted finger anatomy",
      "Smooth, airbrushed skin texture"
    ],
    "likely_prompt": "A high-quality photo of a young blonde man in a flannel shirt and white compression shorts sitting on a stack of weight plates in a gym. Background includes Rogue boxes and a large chalkboard with workout scores. Realistic lighting, gym bro aesthetic, 8k resolution."

### 52. 图像生成提示词：模糊的剪影

**作者**: [路飞 🏴‍☠️ AI 研究员🧐](https://x.com/0xluffy_eth/status/2025058672980992069)  **日期**: 2026-02-21  **语言**: zh

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张图像，其特点是主体在运动中呈现模糊的剪影，强调高对比度、极简构图和动态运动模糊，适用于抽象或街头摄影风格的视觉效果。

![图像生成提示词：模糊的剪影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741703130_bjl0mc_HBp0HmIbgAEVwQ5.jpg)
![图像生成提示词：模糊的剪影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741703111_807guo_HBp0HZjbgAMxQB-.jpg)
![图像生成提示词：模糊的剪影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741703036_zzd3ok_HBp0HNlbgAQIAgw.jpg)
![图像生成提示词：模糊的剪影](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771741703875_g3qgr9_HBp0H2baQAAvJwH.jpg)

```
一个正在运动中的 {argument name="主体" default="主体"} 模糊剪影，穿着 {argument name="颜色" default="颜色"} 的运动服，使用 慢速快门 拍摄，形成强烈的动态拖影效果。
整体为 高对比度、极简构图，画面中 不出现任何 Logo 或文字。
背景保持 中性、干净，风格偏 抽象、有能量感。
整体感觉参考 {argument name="品牌" default="品牌"} 的广告视觉 或 街头摄影的编辑风格。
```

**作者**: [Özge Döner](https://x.com/astronomerozge1/status/2024889108095443399)  **日期**: 2026-02-20  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的结构化 JSON 提示，用于生成受《杀死比尔》启发的 16 毫米磨坊电影风格的 8 格网格拼贴画。它指定了刺眼的闪光灯照明、极端的电影颗粒感，以及一个身穿亮黄色运动服、手持带鞘武士刀的女性主体，重点在于原始、地下编辑的能量。

![16 毫米磨坊式电影剪辑网格（《杀死比尔》风格）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1771655067299_0140r3_HBnZ1nCXMAEvRPe.jpg)

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "lofi_digicam_smoky_editorial_8panel_grid_no_text",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.5_KILLBILL_YELLOW_16MM_GRINDHOUSE"
    },

    "input": {
      "mode": "text_to_image",
      "notes": "Revenge-cinema inspired (Kill Bill vibe) 16mm grindhouse fashion editorial collage. Same adult woman, consistent identity across 8 panels. Harsh flash, dirty analog texture, raw underground energy. No text, no logos, no watermark."
    },

    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 4,
        "cols": 2,
        "gutter": "thin_black"
      },
      "sharpness": "gritty_soft",
      "grain": "extreme_16mm"
    },

    "scene": {
      "environment": "plain industrial wall, minimal interior",
      "mood": "violent calm, exploitation cinema mood, underground 2000s energy",
      "style": "16mm grindhouse scan: heavy grain, gate weave, film dirt, scratches, frame burn on 1-2 panels, uneven exposure, green-yellow color cast, harsh direct flash, slight motion smear"
    },

    "subject": {
      "person": "adult woman",
      "wardrobe": "bright yellow fitted tracksuit with black side stripes, slightly wrinkled texture under harsh flash",
      "hair": "tight ponytail or slicked back wet look",
      "makeup": {
        "eyes": "sharp elongated eyeliner, slightly smudged black kohl",
        "lips": "deep red or muted nude (keep consistent)",
        "skin": "raw texture, visible pores, slight shine from flash"
      },
      "nails": "short glossy red or natural",
      "props": "katana sword sheathed only, held downward or resting against shoulder, no attack pose, purely fashion attitude"
    },

    "panel_plan": {
      "continuity": "same identity and styling across all panels",
      "variation": [
        "panel 1: full-body stance, brutal flash pop",
        "panel 2: low angle power pose, deep shadow behind",
        "panel 3: close-up with intense stare, heavy grain emphasis",
        "panel 4: profile silhouette against wall",
        "panel 5: hand gripping scabbard detail (anatomically correct)",
        "panel 6: seated against wall, legs extended, katana sheathed across lap",
        "panel 7: dynamic step forward motion blur",
        "panel 8: extreme close-up eye with gritty contrast"
      ]
    },

    "lighting": {
      "primary": "harsh on-camera flash",
      "contrast": "very high",
      "shadow": "deep crushed blacks",
      "highlight_behavior": "overexposed hot spots on yellow fabric and cheekbones"
    },

    "negative_prompt": "text, watermark, logo, blood, gore, violence, unsheathed blade attack, extra fingers, distorted anatomy, plastic skin, HDR polish, clean modern look, CGI"
  }
}
```

```

0-3 秒：{argument name="场景1" default="泰国公园草坪"}，家长带孩子散步慢跑，亲子同款运动鞋，阳光笑脸
3-6 秒：{argument name="场景2" default="校园操场"}，小朋友跑步、踢球，轻便儿童运动鞋，活泼可爱
6-9 秒：全家一起逛公园、骑单车，舒适运动鞋，轻松自在
9-12 秒：日常上学、出门逛街，亲子穿搭简约干净，鞋子舒适百搭
12-15...
```

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一张四位著名女演员（安娜·德·阿玛斯、米莉·芭比·布朗、萨迪·辛克和西德尼·斯威尼）在阳光普照的热带海滩上摆姿势的半身照片。它详细说明了她们的阶梯式构图、服装（罗纹背心和牛仔布）、黄金时段光线以及电影般效果的相机技术设置。

![四位女演员在热带海滩摆拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770359897586_fu8914_HAYj25TWIAEnPHB.jpg)

```
A medium shot of four famous actresses, {argument name="actress 1" default="Ana de Armas"}, {argument name="actress 2" default="Millie Bobby Brown"}, {argument name="actress 3" default="Sadie Sink"}, and {argument name="actress 4" default="Sydney Sweeney"}, posing together on a sun-drenched tropical beach. They are arranged in a tiered group composition: Sadie Sink is on the left in the foreground making a peace sign and winking; Sydney Sweeney is kneeling in the front right smiling at the camera; Ana de Armas and Millie Bobby Brown stand behind them, smiling warmly.

Wardrobe & Styling
 * Outfits: Casual summer beachwear. Ribbed tank tops in vibrant primary colors (cobalt blue, bright yellow, crisp white, and black) tucked into light-wash high-waisted denim jeans and cargo-style denim pants.
 * Accessories: Minimalist gold jewelry, including small hoop earrings, thin chain necklaces, and several gold and silver wristwatches/bracelets.
 * Hair: Natural summer styles—Sadie with long wavy red hair; Sydney and Millie with sleek, slicked-back ponytails; Ana with soft, layered brunette hair.
Environment & Lighting
 * Setting: A pristine white sand beach with turquoise ocean waves gently lapping the shore in the background. Several tall, leaning coconut palm trees frame the top of the shot against a clear, pale blue sky.
 * Lighting: Bright, natural golden-hour sunlight coming from the side, creating soft highlights on their skin and a warm, glowing atmosphere.
 * Camera Style: Shot on a high-end digital camera (35mm lens), f/2.8 aperture for a slight soft-focus blur on the distant background, sharp focus on the subjects' faces, 8k resolution, cinematic color grading.
Technical Observations
While the image looks very convincing at a glance, it contains several classic AI artifacts that you might want to "prompt out" or fix in future versions:
 * Extra Fingers: Look closely at the hand on Sadie’s shoulder; there are extra digits blending into her hair.
 * Anatomical Merging: The way the arms and torsos overlap in the center is slightly physically impossible.
 * Watch Details: The watches have distorted faces/bands typical of AI-generated text and metal.
```

**作者**: [UG Update](https://x.com/OhajiemoU85445/status/2019002376510751093)  **日期**: 2026-02-04  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细的提示，用于生成一张超逼真的高角度 POV 自拍图像：一位酷似 Billie Eilish 的女性，在晨光中跪在床上，表情俏皮（眨眼、吐舌），并强调真实的皮肤和织物纹理。

```
{
  "prompt_structure": {
    "subject": {
      "demographics": "Young woman {argument name="subject name" default="Billie Eilish"}, roughly early 20s, fair complexion",
      "features": {
        "hair": "Dirty blonde to light brown hair, pulled back into a casual messy low bun or ponytail, sun-illuminated loose strands and flyaways framing the face",
        "eyes": "Blue-grey eyes, right eye winking, left eye open and looking at camera",
        "face": "Playful scrunched nose expression, natural skin texture with visible pores and slight flush",
        "mouth": "Smiling with teeth visible, tongue playfully sticking out to the side"
 }
    },
    "apparel": {
      "upper_body": "Oversized, pale cream or buttery yellow button-down shirt",
      "fabric": "Textured linen or black cotton gauze, slightly wrinkled, translucent quality in bright light",
      "styling": "Casual loungewear style, buttons done up to mid-chest, loose fit"
    },
    "pose_and_action": {
      "type": "High-angle POV selfie",
      "posture": "Kneeling on a bed, leaning slightly forward toward the lens",
      "limbs": "One arm extended holding the camera (out of frame), other arm resting straight down with hand pressed into the soft mattress",
      "dynamic": "Candid, energetic, spontaneous movement"
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "Bedroom or hotel room interior",
      "foreground": "White, plush duvet/bed sheets with realistic folds and compression from weight",
 "background": " blurred wooden nightstand, neutral beige walls, hint of a lamp and personal items, soft domestic setting"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "source": "Strong natural daylight / morning sun coming from top left",
      "quality": "High contrast sunlight creating rim lighting on hair (halo effect) and distinct soft shadows on the face and neck",
      "tone": "Warm, golden hour or bright morning ambiance"
    },
    "camera_specifications": {
      "angle": "High-angle selfie perspective",
      "lens": "Wide-angle smartphone lens simulation (approx 24mm or 28mm)",
      "aperture": "f/2.2 for slight depth of field blurring the background while keeping face sharp",
      "focus": "Sharp focus on facial expression"
    },
    "style_and_mood": {
      "vibe": "Playful, intimate, silly, carefree, 'woke up like this', goofy aesthetics",
      "aesthetic": "Naturalism, Gen Z selfie style, soft-focus background, clean core"
    },
"tech_specs": {
      "quality": "Ultra photorealistic, 8k resolution, raw photo style",
      "details": "High fidelity skin texture, realistic fabric weave, physically correct lighting rendering, granular detail on eyelashes and hair"
    }
  }
}
```

### 84. 微型水墨运动图像生成提示

**作者**: [踏雪寻仙](https://x.com/TaXue2025/status/2018133978851746147)  **日期**: 2026-02-02  **语言**: zh

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示，用于生成“微型水墨运动”风格的图像。该提示指定了颜色（主导主色、柔和的辅助色）、环境（抽象画布、水墨、极简笔触）、主体（姿态生动的超写实微缩人物、精准的运动服）、构图（严格的俯视图、无透视畸变、图形化布局）和光照（柔和的影棚光、均匀的顶部光照）等方面的约束。

![微型水墨运动图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100849764_7fr12d_HAHaJLAbAAAvfDr.jpg)
![微型水墨运动图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100849769_6tp7g2_HAHaJN_bQAAN2EN.jpg)
![微型水墨运动图像生成提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1770100849838_pdfxtq_HAHaJO-bgAAa_hV.jpg)

```
{
  "色彩": {
    "色彩行为": "主色调主导，辅以极柔和的第二色点缀",
    "饱和度": "中高饱和度，柔化处理，绝不刺眼或浑浊"
  },
  "环境": {
    "世界类型": "抽象的画布表面",
    "材质": [
      "水墨颜料",
      "微妙的调色刀纹理",
      "极简笔触",
      "轻薄的颜料堆叠肌理"
    ],
    "表现规则": "环境以克制的色彩、干净的质感和可控的颜料厚度象征性地表现运动场地或竞技场——绝不追求字面意义上的写实",
    "背景风格": "平静、均匀的色彩块，带有微妙的颜料肌理"
  },
  "主体": {
    "比例": "微缩模型",
    "外观": "{argument name="外观" default="高度写实的人物形象"}",
    "活动": "{argument name="活动" default="运动中的动态瞬间"}",
    "服装": "精准的运动专用服装与装备",
    "姿态风格": "自然、运动中的姿态",
    "阴影": "柔和、微妙的阴影直接投射在主体下方，强化俯视视角"
  },
  "构图": {
    "镜头角度": "严格俯视",
    "镜头朝向": "与表面完全垂直（90度正上方视角）",
    "透视规则": [
      "无倾斜",
      "无对角角度",
      "无透视变形",
      "无景深透视"
    ],
    "布局": "图形化、编辑感、简洁几何",
    "负空间": "刻意且充裕",
    "景深": "扁平的、海报式景深"
  },

### 88. 使用 Tiny Workers 进行图像到图像的转换

**作者**: [Sharon Riley](https://x.com/Just_sharon7/status/2017591558389043643)  **日期**: 2026-01-31  **语言**: en

> 一个用于图像到图像转换的结构化 JSON 提示，指示模型在添加微小的人类工人执行特定动作（如清扫颜料或滚动油漆）时，保留原始图像的背景和颜色，并保持缓慢、自然的运动风格。

![使用 Tiny Workers 进行图像到图像的转换](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769927661665_ps3l7i_G__szH7bEAMUG0H.jpg)

```
{
  "base_image": "use_uploaded_image_exactly_as_is",
  "instructions": {
    "preserve": {
      "background": true,
      "colors": true,
      "shadows": true,
      "water": true,
      "sand": true,
      "palette": true
    },
    "subjects": [
      {
        "type": "tiny_human_worker",
        "actions": [
          {"action": "sweep", "target": "pigment"},
          {"action": "roll_paint", "target": "color_blocks"},
          {"action": "climb", "target": "ladder", "careful": true},
          {"action": "carry", "object": "small_bucket", "place_down": true},
          {"action": "fix_edge", "tool": "brush", "target": "color_block"}
        ],
        "movement_style": "small_natural_slow"
      }
    ],
    "effects": {
      "special_effects": false,
      "light_effects": false,
      "glow": false,
      "smoke": false
    },
    "camera": {
      "movement": false
    },
    "objects": {
      "add": false
    },
    "text": {
      "add": false
    },
    "sound": false
  }
}
```

### 89. 名人图片数据库提示结构

**作者**: [Bahar azam](https://x.com/BaharAzamm561/status/2017386283136643582)  **日期**: 2026-01-30  **语言**: en

> 一个结构化的 JSON 提示词，可作为数据库或指令集，用于生成特定名人（Sydney Sweeney 和 Ana de Armas）在各种预定义场景、服装和情绪下的图像，重点是用于社交媒体内容的高清写实主义。

![名人图片数据库提示结构](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841123139_lcuxmv_G_8yH-ZaUAAbA6a.jpg)
![名人图片数据库提示结构](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841123216_zcfrny_G_8yH9BaYAAW06g.jpg)
![名人图片数据库提示结构](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841123159_60s96h_G_8yH-ZbEAEyZKJ.jpg)
![名人图片数据库提示结构](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769841123522_36nbu2_G_8yH9AbIAA4q1L.jpg)

```
{
  "celebrity_image_database": {
    "subject_1": {
      "name": "{argument name="subject 1 name" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
      "visual_data": [
        {
          "scene_type": "Summer Boat Trip",
          "setting": "Speedboat on a sunny lake, forest background",
          "outfit": "Black and white athletic zip-up wetsuit",
          "features": "Blonde beach waves, chunky black sunglasses",
          "mood": "Playful and laughing"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Cinematic Indoor",
          "setting": "Dimly lit indoor staircase",
          "outfit": "Hot pink cut-out swimsuit",
          "props": "Holding a glass bottle with blue liquid",
          "hair_style": "Blonde hair with thin face-framing braids"
        }
      ]
    },
    "subject_2": {
      "name": "{argument name="subject 2 name" default="Ana de Armas"}",
      "visual_data": [
        {
          "scene_type": "High-Fashion Editorial",
          "setting": "Luxury lounge, black leather sofa, neon blue and pink background",
          "outfit": "Red sequined blazer and matching skirt, black silk inner",
          "jewelry": "Layered gold necklaces, multiple gold bangles",
          "pose": "Sitting elegantly leaning on a round black table"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Outdoor Garden",
          "setting": "Lush tropical greenery, wicker sofa with white cushions",
          "outfit": "Yellow and blue patterned strapless dress, magenta heels",
          "props": "Lime green champagne bucket with bottles"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Candid/Fan Interaction",
          "setting": "Rainy street, under a black umbrella",
          "outfit": "White button-up blouse with decorative buttons",
          "hair_style": "Dark hair in a messy elegant updo"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Beach Lifestyle",
          "setting": "Ocean waves in the background",
          "outfit": "White high-waisted bikini with pineapple print top",
          "accessories": "Round sunglasses, blue beaded bracelet"
        },
        {
          "scene_type": "Casual Outdoor",
          "setting": "Sitting on green grass, white wall background",
          "outfit": "Mustard yellow off-the-shoulder top, floral embroidered shorts",
          "hair_style": "Sleek high ponytail"
        }
      ]
    },
    "technical_meta": {
      "image_quality": "High-definition, realistic",
      "platform_focus": "Social media content creation (Twitter/Instagram)",
      "target_year": "2026"
    }
  }
}
```

### 92. 超逼真健身房锻炼提示（JSON 结构）

**作者**: [Emma](https://x.com/emmagpt0/status/2016842006861918536)  **日期**: 2026-01-29  **语言**: en

> 一个高度详细、结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于 Nano Banana Pro 生成一张超逼真的女性运动员在现代健身房进行杠铃深蹲的抓拍照片。它包括了关于拍摄对象外貌、服装、相机设置（iPhone 15 Pro Max）、灯光，甚至物理模拟（强调汗水和肌肉张力）的具体细节，以实现真实感。

![超逼真健身房锻炼提示（JSON 结构）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755053344_y4vwhh_G_1Cyr8WAAEUgEP.jpg)
![超逼真健身房锻炼提示（JSON 结构）](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1769755053436_g7af8h_G_1Cyr5W0AAIvk8.jpg)

```
{
  "scene": {
    "location": "modern gym interior",
    "environment": {
      "equipment": ["squat rack", "barbell with weight plates", "dumbbells background"],
      "floor": "rubber gym flooring",
      "background": "blurred dumbbell racks, mirrors, LED ceiling lights",
      "atmosphere": "clean, premium fitness studio"
    }
  },

  "subject": {
    "identity_continuity": true,
    "gender": "female",
    "age_range": "20-30",
    "body_type": "athletic, fit, defined muscles",
    "chest_measurement": "90 cm",
    "pose": "{argument name="pose" default="barbell squat, mid-rep, knees bent, barbell on shoulders"}",
    "facial_expression": "painful strain, eyes squeezed, teeth clenched",
    "hair": {
      "color": "platinum blonde",
      "style": "messy high ponytail with loose strands"
    },
    "skin": {
      "texture": "natural pores visible",
      "sweat": "sweat droplets on forehead, chest, shoulders",
      "specular_highlight_map": "subtle skin shine from perspiration"
    }
  },

  "clothing": {
    "top": {
      "type": "sports bra",
      "cut": "deep cleavage neckline",
      "color": "{argument name="top color" default="dark green"}",
      "fabric": "stretch athletic fabric, slightly glossy from sweat"
    },
    "bottom": {
      "type": "mini gym shorts / tight leggings style",
      "color": "dark green",
      "fit": "high-waist, compression fit, accentuating hips and legs"
    },
    "footwear": {
      "type": "training sneakers",
      "color": "black with white sole"
    }
  },

  "physics_simulation": {
    "breast_physics": {
      "gravity": true,
      "inertia": true,
      "compression": true,
      "micro_movement": "subtle natural deformation during squat"
    },
    "muscle_simulation": {
      "muscle_contraction": true,
      "vein_detail": "visible veins on arms and shoulders",
      "tension_map": "quadriceps, glutes, deltoids, traps under load"
    }
  },

  "camera": {
    "device": "iPhone 15 Pro Max",
    "lens": "main wide lens",
    "focal_length_equivalent": "24mm",
    "aperture": "f/1.8",
    "angle": "slightly low angle, eye-level framing",
    "framing": "medium full body, centered subject"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "gym LED overhead lighting",
    "style": "natural imperfect indoor lighting",
    "shadows": "soft directional shadows under chin and muscles",
    "highlights": "specular highlights on sweaty skin"
  },

  "image_style": {
    "aesthetic": "candid iPhone premium lifestyle snapshot",
    "processing": "minimal post-processing, realistic tone mapping",
    "grain": "subtle fine grain for realism",
    "focus": "slight background blur, subject sharp",
    "color_grading": "cool neutral tones, high contrast fitness look"
  },

**作者**: [两斤](https://x.com/0x00_Krypt/status/2012785099822202999)  **日期**: 2026-01-18  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一个 2.5D 等距剖面图，描绘一栋漂浮在星空下的多层模块化公寓楼。该提示详细描述了每一层的内容（音乐室、客厅、厨房、健身房、卧室）、灯光（温暖的琥珀色光芒与深邃的午夜蓝色形成对比），以及所需的艺术风格（扁平矢量、几何线条、Behance 风格、正交视图）。

![浮动模块化公寓楼的等距剖面图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768804327423_y5qzp0_G-7ZS6nWkAAx6b3.jpg)

```
A detailed 2.5D isometric cross-section illustration of a stacked, multi-level modular apartment building floating against a dark navy starry sky. The structure resembles a vertical honeycomb or treehouse, with stylized bare tree branches supporting the rooms at the bottom.

**Detailed Room Contents:**
* **Top Level:** A music room with a black grand piano; an adjacent open balcony where a man stands playing a violin under a bright crescent moon.
* **Upper-Mid Level:** A cozy living room where a woman hugs a black cat; a balcony filled with potted plants and a large white Samoyed dog sitting peacefully.
* **Lower-Mid Level:** A modern kitchen with a chef cooking with steaming pots; a pantry area with a white fridge; a room with an indoor teepee tent decorated with string lights (indoor camping).
* **Bottom Level:** A living room with a crackling fireplace and a man relaxing in an armchair; a gym room with a person on a stationary bike; a bedroom with a red duvet and a reading lamp.

**Lighting & Atmosphere:**
Deep midnight blue background representing the cold night air, contrasting sharply with the warm, inviting amber and orange glow spilling from the interior rooms.

**Art Style:**
Flat vector illustration, clean geometric lines, architectural visualization, orthographic view, vibrant colors, matte finish, Behance style, high definition. --ar 1:1
```

> 一个高度具体的提示，旨在为角色设计或 3D 建模目的，创建一名年轻成年女性的四视图参考图（正面、左侧面、右侧面、背面）。它要求采用纯白色背景和极简服装，以清晰展示详细的身体比例和肌肉线条。

![用于 3D 建模的四视图角色参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468610961_c2a45y_G-pSqcEawAADeXq.jpg)
![用于 3D 建模的四视图角色参考图](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768468611783_zia0py_G-pSpm2WEAAj7Wg.png)

```
Create a detailed and realistic full-body reference image on a plain white background, showing four views of the young adult woman in the attached image, follow this description:

    "body_description": 
      "ethnicity": "caucasian with fair skin tone"
      "hair": brown with blonde highlights, long, wavy",
      "build": "athletic hourglass, fit and toned",
      "torso": "narrow, high-waisted, plain stomach",
      "bust": "proportional, firm",
      "waist": "taut, slim, high-definition transition to hips",
      "hips": "wide, curvy, pronounced shelf-like curve at the iliac crest",
      "legs": "toned, athletic thighs with smooth skin transition",

Arrange the views horizontally from left to right: front view, left side profile view, right side profile view, and back view. In each pose, she stands straight with arms relaxed at her sides, feet slightly apart, wearing a simple black sports bra and black thong underwear to clearly display body proportions, muscle definition, facial details, hair, and posture. Ensure a 4:4 aspect ratio, high resolution, realistic rendering, no shadows, no additional elements, and equal spacing between views for easy reference.
```

### 120. 编辑平铺时尚图片生成器

**作者**: [Aimi Kōda](https://x.com/aimikoda/status/2011204986865156287)  **日期**: 2026-01-13  **语言**: en

> 一个高度受限的提示模板，旨在生成高分辨率、具有编辑风格的平铺时尚图像，严格采用俯视视角，纯粹专注于服装排列，不描绘或暗示任何人体或体积。

![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900552_gokym2_G-k7N_aW8AA2kuf.jpg)
![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900638_xtp8pr_G-k7MC1WIAIruWa.jpg)
![编辑平铺时尚图片生成器](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768466900934_thdzb4_G-k7M47X0AEGCba.jpg)

```
[OUTFIT_STYLE] = Use the outfit from the reference image | casual utilitarian womenswear | casual mens streetwear
[COMPOSITION_SCHEME] = seated-inspired angular layout | standing-inspired vertical layout | walking-inspired offset layout | dynamic diagonal layout | balance-inspired asymmetric layout | editorial flat-lay grid break | sculptural negative-space layout | yoga-inspired angular balance layout | athletic-inspired directional layout
[SURFACE] = clean matte studio backdrop | soft neutral paper surface | cool tone matte backdrop
[ACCESSORY_MODE] = outfit_integrated | decorative | none

Make a high resolution flat lay fashion image for editorial and catalog use.
Use a strict top down camera angle with a natural 50mm equivalent perspective and perfectly parallel framing.
Set the scene on [SURFACE] with no visible texture seams or edge shadows.

Show only clothing items and approved accessories placed on the surface.
Do not depict or imply any human body, body parts, limbs, skin, joints, or anatomy.
Do not include legs, hips, feet, knees, or any biological structure.

Arrange garments as a flat, uninhabited composition following [COMPOSITION_SCHEME].
Interpret [COMPOSITION_SCHEME] purely as a geometric layout logic, never as a body configuration.
Use angles, spacing, and directional alignment only to suggest balance and posture.

Keep every garment fully flat with zero internal volume.
Force all bottom garments including pants or leggings to remain collapsed, empty, and tension-free.
Do not stretch, contour, wrap, or compress fabric.
Represent bends only through sharp planar folds and angular breaks.
Prohibit smooth curves, rounded forms, seated volume, or body-fit deformation.

Allow folds and wrinkles only as gravity-driven surface creases.
Ensure clothing reads strictly as laid fabric, not worn, inhabited, or shaped by a body.

Select garments and accessories based on {argument name="outfit style" default="OUTFIT_STYLE"}.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is outfit_integrated, include only functionally worn items.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is decorative, allow accessories as independent flat objects.
If [ACCESSORY_MODE] is none, exclude all accessories entirely.

Use soft diffused daylight from above with gentle shadows directly beneath each item.
Keep spacing balanced with visible negative space around the composition.
Avoid mannequins, models, body silhouettes, stuffing, air filled shapes, extra items, text, logos, or branding.
Ensure clarity, accurate fabric texture, and a calm contemporary aesthetic.
```

### 124. 用于地板平衡瑜伽摄影的结构化 JSON 提示

**作者**: [Cuties](https://x.com/cuties7377/status/2010313094891798567)  **日期**: 2026-01-11  **语言**: en

> 一个全面的 JSON 提示，旨在生成专注于高级地面平衡瑜伽姿势的高端编辑级健身摄影。它详细描述了拍摄对象的体格、姿势细节（受控保持、核心发力）、服装、简约的影棚环境、柔和的影棚灯光以及相机细节，以实现宁静、强劲且适合病毒式健康内容传播的编辑级图像。

![用于地板平衡瑜伽摄影的结构化 JSON 提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768225946605_8w97fa_G-YRGKQX0AApaZE.jpg)

```
{

 "viral floor balance fitness post",

"lean, flexible, strong core",

 "calm, confident, grounded"
  },

    "leg_position": 
"one or both legs lifted or extended with balance",
    "spine_alignment": 
"elongated spine with controlled arch or neutral line",

"tight core visibly supporting balance",
    "balance_quality": 
"stable, effortless, graceful"
  },

 "calm focus with inner strength",

    "micro_details":
 "relaxed jaw, composed facial muscles"
  },
  "wardrobe": {

### 125. 生成爆款运动跳跃定格照片的详细 JSON 提示词

**作者**: [Cuties](https://x.com/cuties7377/status/2010225997463834883)  **日期**: 2026-01-11  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，专为 AI 图像生成器（可能是 Gemini Nano Pro）设计，用于创建一张电影级、高冲击力的照片，内容是一位运动型女性身体正在表演“跳跃定格”姿势。该提示详细说明了内容目标、视觉风格、动作概念、姿势、主体体格、服装、环境和专业影棚灯光等要求，以确保生成一张超逼真、编辑级、适合在社交媒体上病毒式传播的图片。

### 127. 8K 名人监控录像

**作者**: [Selena 🔥](https://x.com/Queen_khan143/status/2009612442876412186)  **日期**: 2026-01-09  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的提示，旨在模拟 8K 闭路电视（CCTV）画面，内容是四位特定名人（Sydney Sweeney、Ana de Armas、Margot Robbie、Scarlett Johansson）在繁忙的城市街道上行走，画面中包含数字伪影，如白色人脸检测框、低对比度，以及用于增强清晰度的放大插图。

{

    "type": "CCTV footage",
    "settings": {
      "camera_angle": "high-angle overhead",
      "style": "cool muted tones, low contrast, soft digital grain, mild daylight shadows, subtle lens distortion, slight barrel effect"
    },
    "subjects": [
      { "name": "{argument name="subject 1" default="Sydney Sweeney"}", "hair": "long blonde", "outfit": "oversized red shirt", "expression": "neutral/focused" },
      { "name": "Ana de Armas", "hair": "medium brown", "outfit": "black jacket", "expression": "alert" },
      { "name": "Margot Robbie", "hair": "blonde tied back", "outfit": "light denim top", "expression": "focused" },
      { "name": "Scarlett Johansson", "hair": "red loose", "outfit": "dark casual wear", "expression": "neutral" }
    ],
    "action": { "movement": "fast walk left to right", "position": "centered", "spacing": "even", "motion_blur": "subtle", "footsteps_shadows": "visible" },
    "background": "busy urban street, pedestrians blurred with bokeh, daylight shadows, reflections on wet pavement, distant signage slightly distorted",
    "face_detection": { "boxes": "white rectangles around faces", "accuracy": "medium-high", "highlight_edges": "soft" },
    "zoom_inset": { "focus": "all faces", "clarity": "enhanced", "brightness": "slightly corrected", "zoom_ratio": 2.5, "position": "bottom-right" },
    "composition": { "depth_of_field": "shallow on group, strong background blur", "frame_balance": "center-weighted", "perspective_lines": "slightly converging" },

### 132. 前卫运动风：腾空而起的冰冻体操运动员

**作者**: [Cuties](https://x.com/cuties7377/status/2007753776367620494)  **日期**: 2026-01-04  **语言**: en

> 一个高度技术化的提示，用于生成一张超详细的 12k 分辨率图像，捕捉一位精英体操运动员在复杂动作中腾空而起的瞬间。它强调“粗野主义极简”风格、戏剧性的低角度构图、高对比度边缘照明，以及冷色调频闪效果，以完美凝固动作，突出肌肉线条、汗珠和哑光黑色紧身衣的质感。

![前卫运动风：腾空而起的冰冻体操运动员](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767606957548_j9pfv7_G9zxG9CWgAASsnJ.jpg)

```
{

  },

      "depth_of_field": "Deep focus on the subject with a motion-blurred peripheral background"
    },

    },
    "facial_details": {
      "expression": "Intense focus; 'the zone'; jaw slightly clenched, eyes sharp and directed toward the landing point",

    },

  },

    "environment": [
      "chaotic background with paparazzi cameras",
      "red velvet ropes",

      "dark night sky contrast"
    ],
    "atmosphere": "electric, exclusive, superstar energy"
  },

  "lighting": {
    "type": "Direct Flash (Paparazzi Style)",
    "effect": "High contrast hard light, glistening skin, sharp shadows behind the subject, bright reflections on dress"
  },

  "subject": {

    },
    "pose": {

    },

      "jewelry": "Diamond choker, large stud earrings"
    }
  },

### 136. 舒适傍晚：组合沙发上的生活方式摄影

**作者**: [Asher](https://x.com/Nooreman1k/status/2007382899495186912)  **日期**: 2026-01-03  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 提示，用于使用 Gemini Nano Banana Pro 生成一张温馨、私密的居家生活照片。场景设定在傍晚的现代客厅，一位女性身穿酒红色休闲套装，躺在奶油色组合沙发上，周围是柔和温暖的灯光，并摆放着爆米花和蜡烛等道具。

```
{
  "image_prompt_structure": {
    "meta": {
      "type": "Lifestyle Photography",
      "aspect_ratio": "16:9",
      "mood": "Cozy, Intimate, Relaxed"
    },
    "scene_setup": {
      "location": "Modern living room",
      "time_of_day": "Evening",
      "lighting": {
        "type": "Soft warm indoor",
        "sources": ["Ambient room lighting", "Candlelight accents"],
        "quality": "Evenly distributed, glowing"
      },
      "camera": {
        "angle": "High-angle / Slightly elevated",
        "focus": "Subject in foreground",
        "perspective": "Looking down toward the sofa"
      }
    },
    "subject": {
      "demographics": {
        "gender": "Female-presenting",
        "age_appearance": "Young adult to adult"
      },
      "appearance": {
        "hair": {
          "color": "Light brown with blonde highlights",
          "style": "Loose, voluminous waves",
          "parting": "Side-parted"
        },
        "makeup": {
          "skin": "Smooth, contoured finish",
          "eyes": "Defined brows and lashes",
          "lips": "Full lips, neutral-toned lipstick"
        },
        "expression": "Neutral to soft, relaxed eyes, slight smile",
        "gaze": "Direct eye contact with camera"
      },
      "attire": {
        "item": "Matching lounge set",
        "color": "Deep burgundy / Wine red",
        "fabric": "Soft, slightly shimmery",
        "fit": "Form-fitting",
        "details": {
          "top": "Long-sleeve",
          "bottom": "Full-length fitted pants",
          "feet": "Barefoot"
        }
      },
      "pose": {
        "main_position": "Lying on side on sectional sofa",
        "body_orientation": "Three-quarter view, torso angled to camera",
        "limbs": {
          "legs": "Bent and stacked, feet resting naturally",
          "arms": "Relaxed, hands resting gently in front",

### 137. Luxury Streetwear Instagram Feed Composite

**作者**: [Willy](https://x.com/jw660227/status/2006738251101741458)  **日期**: 2026-01-01  **语言**: en

> A detailed, structured prompt for creating a high-fashion Instagram feed composite (4:5 ratio) featuring a stunning Eurasian model in a luxury/streetwear fusion outfit (silk slip dress and high-top sneakers). The layout is an irregular grid with overlapping images, set on an urban rooftop at sunset, emphasizing dynamic elements like swirling gold dust and dramatic lighting.

![Luxury Streetwear Instagram Feed Composite](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767508388988_59sfas_G9ldzH2bMAAIUDg.jpg)

```
Stunning Eurasian (Chinese/French) model, Instagram feed, 4:5 ratio.

LAYOUT: Irregular Grid (main image 60% of space, details filling remaining) + Layered (images overlapping for depth).

DIRECTION: Diagonal flow guiding eye from top left to bottom right.

BACKGROUND: Urban rooftop at sunset with blurred city lights, graffiti art accents, high-fashion editorial vibe.

PRODUCT: Worn shot – model showcasing silver high-top sneakers with pink accents, close-up detail shots of sneaker texture and design layered over main image.

DYNAMIC: Gold dust particles swirling around sneakers and model, fabric of dress floating dramatically, light rays catching the gold dust.

TONE: Color contrast – cool silver sneakers against warm sunset backdrop, pink accents popping against the urban gray.

STYLE: Luxury + Streetwear fusion. Model in {argument name="dress type" default="silk slip dress with lace trim"}, diamond jewelry, and messy high ponytail. Raw urban setting juxtaposed with high-end fashion elements.

UI ELEMENTS: None.

CAMERA: Hasselblad H6D, 85mm f/1.2, dramatic rim lighting with soft fill, composite shot.

Style keywords: streetwear meets luxury, unexpected elegance, golden hour glow, urban fairytale.. A stylish handwritten signature Willy is elegantly and small letters placed at the Bottom Right corner
```

### 143. 热带网红美学与刺眼的正午阳光

**作者**: [Dominus the Prompter](https://x.com/AkatsokK/status/2005305839003873723)  **日期**: 2025-12-28  **语言**: en

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细 JSON 提示词，用于模拟在热带度假村环境中用 iPhone Pro Max 拍摄的照片。该提示词强调正午烈日下极高的对比度光线，营造出深邃、压实的黑色阴影，并戏剧性地勾勒出一位身穿比基尼的健美女性的身体轮廓，以实现“网红生活方式美学”，同时保留可见的数字噪点和真实的皮肤纹理。

    "environment": "Tight vertical medium shot at an affluent tropical resort. Background features intense emerald green lush foliage, a dark palm tree trunk, and rustic wooden cabana structure with slatted shutters.",
    "lighting": "Harsh, midday tropical direct sunlight. Extreme high-contrast lighting, producing deep, crushed black shadows that dramatically contour the body. Smart HDR stress test, resulting in near-blown-out highlights on the white bikini fabric.",
    "camera_gear": "Shot on iPhone 16 Pro Max, Main Camera 24mm f/1.78, simulating 2x optical zoom for tight compression. Slightly low angle framing.",
    "processing": "Apple ProRAW color science, ultra-sharp detail from Deep Fusion, high saturation and warm bronze color grading, {argument name="aesthetic style" default="Influencer Lifestyle aesthetic"}.",
    "imperfections": "Intense digital noise visible within the crushed black shadows, authentic skin texture and pores visible, high contrast, minimal digital artifacting common in heavy mobile HDR processing."
  },
  "full_prompt_string": "Shot on iPhone 16 Pro Max, 9:16 vertical ratio, influential tropical luxury aesthetic.   "negative_prompt": "professional camera, studio lighting, DSLR, bokeh balls, anamorphic lens, low dynamic range, low saturation, blurry, vintage film grain, smooth skin, cinema lighting, painting, illustration, cartoon"

### 145. Off-White × Timberland Industrial Work Alpine Parka 编辑提示

**作者**: [Sienna](https://x.com/siennalovesai/status/2003887474548842706)  **日期**: 2025-12-24  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 格式提示，专为图像生成模型（Gemini Nano Banana Pro）设计，用于创建一张粗犷、潮酷的户外时尚编辑图片。主体是一位年轻女性，身穿概念款 Off-White x Timberland 多功能滑雪派克大衣，将高端街头时尚与工业工装美学融为一体。

### 153. 每周穿搭造型手册生成

**作者**: [シュナプーン](https://x.com/schnapoon/status/2001847957390549090)  **日期**: 2025-12-19  **语言**: ja

> 这是一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的详细提示，用于根据参考图片的风格生成每周服装搭配指南。它会为指定的角色和主题创建一份为期 7 天的时尚搭配，在保持一致性的同时展示七套不同的服装。输出内容为杂志风格的版式，并为每一天标注了特定的文本标签。

![每周穿搭造型手册生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238191867_8md5q8_G8fwUNwaAAA-ALc.jpg)
![每周穿搭造型手册生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238192599_9k9qi2_G8fwU2laAAAsmaj.jpg)
![每周穿搭造型手册生成](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766238193781_g06peo_G8fwVZSa0AAkGC7.jpg)

```
# 設定項目（ここを変更してください）
設定:
[キャラクターの特徴]: {argument name="キャラクターの特徴" default="黒髪ロングヘアの女子高生"}
[ファッションのテーマ]: {argument name="ファッションのテーマ" default="現代女子高生の普段着、清楚系"}

変換のルール:
- [キャラクターの特徴] の同一人物が、横一列に7人並んでいるファッションルックブックの画像。
- [ファッションのテーマ] に基づいた、それぞれ異なる7種類の新しい私服コーディネートのみを着用している。
- 参照画像の [画風・スタイル] を完全に維持している。
- [参照画像の衣装] は着用せず、[ファッションのテーマ] に基づいた、それぞれ異なる7種類のコーディネートを着ている。
- 全身ショット。
- 背景は真っ白、もしくはわずかにアイボリー。
- 足元には自然な影が落ちている。画像のレイアウトは雑誌の切り抜きのよう。
- 各人物の下には左から順に「Monday」「Tuesday」「Wednesday」「Thursday」「Friday」「Saturday」「Sunday」という文字が書かれている。
- 上部にはスタイリッシュなタイトルテキスト。

アートスタイル:
- 高解像
- スタジオライティング
- 4k
- --ar 16:9
```

### 159. 基于认知科学的高点击率缩略图设计提示

**作者**: [Maki@Sunwood AI Labs.](https://x.com/hAru_mAki_ch/status/1999484851594879441)  **日期**: 2025-12-12  **语言**: ja

> 一个为 Nano Banana Pro 设计的复杂系统提示，旨在根据认知科学（神经科学、心理学、行为经济学）原理创建高点击率（CTR）的缩略图。它指示 AI 采用专业艺术总监的角色，分析输入文本，并在绘图前遵循详细的思考过程（思考模式），重点关注面部激活、突出效果和最小化认知负荷。它还包括具体的设计和排版说明。

![基于认知科学的高点击率缩略图设计提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765991038145_9u0j8h_G7-Xmu7akAAgBN1.jpg)

```
あなたは、認知科学（神経科学、心理学、行動経済学）の知見をクリエイティブに統合する「適応的顕著性モデル」の専門家であり、トップクラスのアートディレクターです。

最後に提供される【入力テキスト（記事のタイトルや冒頭）】を深く分析し、その記事のCTR（クリック率）を最大化するサムネイル画像を生成してください。

もし参照画像が添付されている場合は、そのキャラクターを「記事の内容をプレゼンする人物」として配置し、一貫性を維持してください。

▼ 生成プロセスへの指示 (Thinking Process)
Nano Banana Proの「思考モード（Thinking Mode）」を使用し、描画前に以下のステップで論理的に構成案を練ってください。

1.  **[ステップ1: コンテンツ分析とフックの抽出]**
    * 入力テキストから「読者が得られる最大の利益（ベネフィット）」または「知らなければ損をするリスク（損失回避）」を特定する（プロスペクト理論の適用）。
    * 記事のテーマを象徴する、最も直感的な視覚メタファー（例：上昇、鍵、雷、光、闇など）を選定する。

2.  **[ステップ2: 適応的顕著性モデルによる最適化]**
    * **FFA活性化 (Face Fusiform Area)**: キャラクターの顔、特に「目」の解像度を最大化し、視聴者と視線が合う（アイコンタクト）ように構図を設計する。表情は記事のトーン（驚き、自信、深刻さなど）に合わせる。
    * **ポップアウト効果 (Pop-out Effect)**: 背景色と補色関係にある「鮮烈な色（ネオンカラーや黄色など）」を、タイトルテキストや重要アイコンに使用し、視覚的な突出を作る。
    * **認知負荷理論 (Cognitive Load)**: 情報を詰め込みすぎない。「1つの顔 + 1つのインパクトあるテキスト + 1つの背景メタファー」に要素を絞る。

3.  **[ステップ3: レイアウト設計]**
    * Zの法則やFの法則を意識し、視線が「顔」→「高ジャンプ率のテキスト」→「クリック要素」へ流れるように配置する。

▼ デザイン・スタイル指定
* **構図**: クローズアップ（バストアップ）またはミディアムショット。キャラクターを中央または三分割法の交点に配置。
* **テイスト**: [入力テキストのジャンルに最適化せよ。例：ビジネスなら「洗練された・信頼感」、エンタメなら「鮮やか・高彩度」、技術系なら「サイバーパンク・未来的」]
* **テキストレンダリング（重要）**:
    * 入力テキストから、**最もキャッチーな短いフレーズ（10文字以内推奨）**を抽出する。
    * **フォント**: 「**太字の明朝体（Heavy Serif）**」を使用する。可読性を高めるため、文字には**背景色と対比する「太い縁取り（Thick Outline）」**を必ず施すこと。
    * **配置（ジャンプ率）**: **「ジャンプ率（Jump Rate）」を高く設定する**。メインのキーワードを極端に大きく、助詞やサブ情報を小さく配置し、視覚的なメリハリとリズムを生み出す。
* **キャラクター演出**: 参照キャラクターがいる場合、その服装を記事のテーマ（白衣、スーツ、探検家、カジュアルなど）に合わせて調整する。

▼ 入力テキスト
{argument name="入力テキスト" default="（記事のタイトルとか内容）"}
```

**Related**: [[综合动漫]]、[[赛博朋克]]

### 171. 高定街头服饰：强迫透视时尚大片

> 一个高度技术化且结构化的 JSON 提示词，用于生成多画幅、高级时装街头服饰的专题图片。它侧重于技术执行，包括多画幅一致性、身份锁定（严格执行参考图中的面部特征）、超广角透视研究，以及对模特外貌、服装（霓虹橙色飞行员夹克、战术裤）和材质保真度的详细描述。

![高定街头服饰：强迫透视时尚大片](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765438568512_a0y1h5_G7pFGPuasAAkHP3.jpg)

```
{
  "meta_control": {
    "generation_mode": "multi_panel_consistent",
    "priority_stack": ["identity_lock", "perspective_physics", "material_fidelity", "environmental_coherence"],
    "quality_target": "editorial_print_ready"
  },
  "intent": {
    "primary": "High-fashion streetwear editorial with extreme wide-angle perspective study",
    "secondary": "Technical demonstration of foreshortening and forced perspective",
    "publication_context": "Double-page spread, fashion magazine collage layout"
  },
  "frame": {
    "aspect_ratio": "3:4",
    "layout": {
      "type": "2x2 grid collage",
      "gutter_width": "2px white or seamless",
      "panel_uniformity": "identical dimensions per panel"
    }
  },
  "subject": {
    "type": "Human female fashion model",
    "identity_lock": {
      "enforcement_level": "strict",
      "anchor_features": ["face_geometry", "skin_tone", "body_proportions", "hair_style"]
    },
    "biometrics": {
      "age_presentation": "22-26",
      "height_cm": 175,
      "build": "Slender athletic, model proportions",
      "ethnicity_presentation": "Northern European features"
    },
    "facial_signature": {
      "structure": "Angular diamond face, high cheekbones, defined jawline",
      "eyes": "Sharp almond, steel grey, graphic black winged liner extending 8mm",
      "nose": "Refined, straight, small silver hoop piercing on left nostril",
      "lips": "Natural shape, matte nude-pink",
      "skin": "Fair, visible pores and natural texture, subtle peach fuzz, tiny freckle cluster left cheekbone",
      "expression_default": "Cool confidence, intense direct eye contact, composed"
    },
    "hair": {
      "style": "Platinum blonde straight bob, blunt bangs ending at eyebrows",
      "texture": "Silky, light-catching, individual strand definition",
      "behavior": "Natural movement responding to pose changes"
    },
    "wardrobe": {
      "jacket": {
        "item": "Oversized bomber jacket",
        "material": "Ripstop nylon, high gloss",
        "color": "Neon orange (vivid, saturated)",
        "state": "Unzipped, hanging open",
        "light_behavior": "Sharp specular highlights, visible weave texture"
      },
      "top": {

### 173. 休闲主角与粉色宝马 i8 自拍提示

> 一个高度详细的中文提示，用于生成一张超现实的年轻女性在镀铬粉色宝马 i8 旁自拍的图像。该提示指定了“随性的主角气质”，详细的服装（黄色超短 T 恤，白色迷你运动短裤），铂金色头发，并着重于“泰然自若”的姿势和表情。

### 174. 病毒式幻灯片提示：粉色宝马自拍

**作者**: [gauche](https://x.com/gaucheai/status/1997405140723323255)  **日期**: 2025-12-06  **语言**: en

> 一个高度结构化的 JSON 提示，详细说明了如何生成一张用于幻灯片的逼真图像，内容为一名年轻女子在一辆镀铬粉色宝马 i8 旁自拍，强调了特定的服装、姿势、表情以及“主角光环”美学。

![病毒式幻灯片提示：粉色宝马自拍](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765122630723_d3b5ie_G7g1VriWkAAhtan.jpg)

```
{

### 175. 复古照相亭情侣照片条提示

**作者**: [Kaan](https://x.com/kaanakz/status/1996953465747038568)  **日期**: 2025-12-05  **语言**: en

> 一个详细的 JSON 格式提示，旨在让 Nano Banana 生成一张以一对年轻情侣为主题的垂直照片亭条纹拼贴画。该提示详细说明了构图、取景、服装、四个俏皮浪漫的姿势序列、复古美学、刺眼的闪光灯照明，以及光泽感和时间戳等技术细节。

![复古照相亭情侣照片条提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1765089423051_ygzf6d_G7aal8FWMAA7Bdo.jpg)

```
{
  "image_reference": {
    "source": "attached_female_photo",
    "weight": 0.85,
    "note": "Use the female reference for the woman in the couple"
  },
  "composition": {
    "type": "Vertical Photo Booth Strip (Collage)",
    "layout": "Four vertical frames arranged in a column with white borders",
    "framing": "Waist-up or Close-up shots, tight framing inside the booth",
    "aspect_ratio": "1:3"
  },
  "content": {
    "subjects": {
      "couple": "A young couple ({argument name="woman description" default="Woman from reference"} and a Man)",
      "attire": "{argument name="attire" default="Casual date night outfits, maybe a denim jacket or leather jacket"}"
    },
    "sequence_of_poses": {
      "frame_1": "{argument name="pose 1" default="Standard smiling pose, heads leaning together, looking at lens"}",
      "frame_2": "{argument name="pose 2" default="Funny faces, sticking tongues out or bunny ears, laughing"}",
      "frame_3": "{argument name="pose 3" default="Romantic moment, a kiss on the cheek or looking into each other's eyes"}",
      "frame_4": "{argument name="pose 4" default="Total chaos, laughing uncontrollably, maybe one person looking away or fixing hair"}"
    },
    "background": "{argument name="background" default="Red velvet curtain or metallic textured wall (typical photo booth interior)"}",
    "props": "Maybe holding a prop mustache or glasses in one frame (optional)"
  },
  "atmosphere": {
    "mood": "Romantic, playful, intimate, spontaneous",
    "lighting": "Direct harsh flash photography (front-facing), creating slight shadows on the curtain behind them",
    "aesthetics": "Retro photobooth style, slightly desaturated colors or high contrast black and white (optional), skin texture visible"
  },
  "technical_specs": {
    "camera_simulation": "Photobooth automated camera",
    "finish": "Glossy photo paper texture effect",
    "details": "Timestamp or 'Date' printed digitally in red/orange on the side or between frames (e.g., '2025')"
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "split screen issues",
    "distorted faces",
    "blurry",
    "modern studio lighting",
    "outdoor background",
    "more than 4 frames"
  ]
}
```

### 176. 宿舍日常生活 iPhone 拍摄提示

**作者**: [离谱](https://x.com/CaomuQ625/status/1990985152458338638)  **日期**: 2025-11-19  **语言**: zh

> 描述两名女学生在宿舍里的 iPhone 快照的长提示。

![宿舍日常生活 iPhone 拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886849945_6tgkan_G6Fl-5MaAAAbKXd.jpg)
![宿舍日常生活 iPhone 拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886853291_4a6vpt_G6FmOJzbMAE2Oo6.jpg)
![宿舍日常生活 iPhone 拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886856716_i3wqqf_G6FmaBBaAAEiFje.png)
![宿舍日常生活 iPhone 拍摄提示](https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1763886859624_028llv_G6FmbXLaYAEjR1Z.jpg)

```
iPhone随手拍，宿舍日常场景照片，两位穿着校服的女生坐在双层铁架床的下铺。左侧女生左腿搭床沿、右腿前伸，低头看手机；中间女生双腿弯曲并拢，身体端正。背景为女生宿舍，上铺堆放杂乱衣物，地面散落多双运动鞋、休闲鞋及袜子。低分辨率照片，随手拍，生活化随意氛围，展现宿舍放松日常状态。比例 9:16。
```
